OBJECT Report 11012576 Plant Exploitation
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=;
    Time=;
    Version List=4PS14.00;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=[DEU=Werkzeugnutzung;
               ENU=Plant Exploitation;
               NLD=Materieel exploitatie;
               NOR=Maskinutnyttelse;
               SVE=Maskinutnyttjande];
    OnInitReport=BEGIN
                   PlantSetup.GET;
                   IF NOT PrintColTotalCosts AND NOT PrintColTotalBudget AND NOT PrintColTotalRevenues AND NOT PrintColResult THEN BEGIN
                     PrintColTotalCosts := TRUE;
                     PrintColTotalBudget := TRUE;
                     PrintColTotalRevenues := TRUE;
                     PrintColResult := TRUE;
                   END;

                   IF NOT GroupTotalsLevel1 AND NOT GroupTotalsLevel2 AND NOT GroupTotalsLevel3 AND NOT PrintPerType THEN BEGIN
                     GroupTotalsLevel1 := TRUE;
                     GroupTotalsLevel2 := TRUE;
                     GroupTotalsLevel3 := TRUE;
                     PrintPerType := TRUE;
                   END;
                 END;

    OnPreReport=BEGIN
                  MaxNoColumns := ARRAYLEN(HeaderTxt);
                  Counter := 0;
                  PlantType.COPYFILTER("Cost Component Filter", CostComponent.Code);
                  IF CostComponent.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                    REPEAT
                      Counter := Counter + 1;
                      IF Counter <= MaxNoColumns THEN
                        HeaderTxt[Counter] := CostComponent.Description;
                      IF PrintColRevenues AND PrintCostAndRevOnSameLine THEN BEGIN
                        IF Counter <= MaxNoColumns THEN
                          HeaderTxt[Counter] := HeaderTxt[Counter] + '\' + Text014;
                        Counter := Counter + 1;
                        IF Counter <= MaxNoColumns THEN
                          HeaderTxt[Counter] := CostComponent.Description + '\' + Text017;
                      END;
                    UNTIL CostComponent.NEXT = 0;
                  END;
                  CostComponentColCount := Counter;

                  IF PrintColTotalCosts THEN BEGIN
                    Counter := Counter + 1;
                    IF Counter <= MaxNoColumns THEN BEGIN
                      ColNoTotalCosts := Counter;
                      IF NOT OnlyTotalsOfSelectedCostComp THEN
                        HeaderTxt[ColNoTotalCosts] := Text001
                      ELSE
                        HeaderTxt[ColNoTotalCosts] := Text009;
                    END;
                  END;

                  IF PrintColTotalBudget THEN BEGIN
                    PlantBudget.GET(PlantBudget.Code);
                    Counter := Counter + 1;
                    IF Counter <= MaxNoColumns THEN BEGIN
                      ColNoTotalBudget := Counter;
                      IF NOT OnlyTotalsOfSelectedCostComp THEN
                        HeaderTxt[ColNoTotalBudget] := Text010
                      ELSE
                        HeaderTxt[ColNoTotalBudget] := Text012;
                    END;
                    Counter := Counter + 1;
                    IF Counter <= MaxNoColumns THEN BEGIN
                      ColNoTotalBudgetResult := Counter;
                      IF NOT OnlyTotalsOfSelectedCostComp THEN
                        HeaderTxt[ColNoTotalBudgetResult] := Text011
                      ELSE
                        HeaderTxt[ColNoTotalBudgetResult] := Text013;
                    END;
                  END;

                  IF PrintColTotalRevenues THEN BEGIN
                    Counter := Counter + 1;
                    IF Counter <= MaxNoColumns THEN BEGIN
                      ColNoTotalRevenues := Counter;
                      HeaderTxt[ColNoTotalRevenues] := Text002
                    END;
                  END;

                  IF PrintColResult THEN BEGIN
                    Counter := Counter + 1;
                    IF Counter <= MaxNoColumns THEN BEGIN
                      ColNoResult := Counter;
                      HeaderTxt[ColNoResult] := Text003;
                    END
                  END;

                  IF PrintColOccupation THEN BEGIN
                    Counter := Counter + 1;
                    IF Counter <= MaxNoColumns THEN BEGIN
                      ColNoOccupation := Counter;
                      HeaderTxt[ColNoOccupation] := Text004;
                    END;
                  END;

                  IF Counter > MaxNoColumns THEN
                    ERROR(Text005 + Text007, Counter, MaxNoColumns);
                  IF Counter = 0 THEN
                    ERROR(Text006 + Text007);
                END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 1100525002;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=CONST(1));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               PlantType.DPA_SetFilters(CurrReport.OBJECTID(FALSE));
                             END;
                              }

    { 1100525001;1;Column;COMPANYNAME        ;
               SourceExpr=COMPANYPROPERTY.DISPLAYNAME }

    { 1100525000;1;Column;REPORTNAME         ;
               SourceExpr=GetReportName }

    { 1100525005;1;Column;REPORTFILTER       ;
               SourceExpr=GetReportFilter }

    { 1100528747;1;Column;PrintPerType       ;
               SourceExpr=PrintPerType }

    { 1100528748;1;Column;PrintPerNo         ;
               SourceExpr=PrintPerNo }

    { 1100528775;1;Column;PrintRevenues      ;
               SourceExpr=PrintColRevenues }

    { 1100528750;1;Column;PrintColBudgetPerCostComp;
               SourceExpr=PrintColBudgetPerCostComp }

    { 1100528752;1;Column;PrintCostAndRevOnSameLine;
               SourceExpr=PrintCostAndRevOnSameLine }

    { 1100528749;1;Column;ColNoOccupation    ;
               SourceExpr=ColNoOccupation }

    { 1100529600;1;Column;CostComponentColCount;
               SourceExpr=CostComponentColCount }

    { 1100525004;;DataItem;PlantType         ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012551;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Group Level 1,Group Level 2,Group Level 3);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               DPA_SetFilters(CurrReport.OBJECTID(FALSE));
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  CLEAR(GroupLevelTxt);
                                  IF ("Group Level 1" <> '') AND ("Group Level 1" <> GroupLevel.Code) THEN
                                    IF GroupLevel.GET("Group Level 1") THEN
                                      IF (GroupLevel.Description <> '') THEN
                                        GroupLevelTxt[1] := GroupLevel.Description;

                                  IF ("Group Level 2" <> '') AND ("Group Level 2" <> GroupLevel.Code) THEN
                                    IF GroupLevel.GET("Group Level 2") THEN
                                      IF (GroupLevel.Description <> '') THEN
                                        GroupLevelTxt[2] := GroupLevel.Description;

                                  IF ("Group Level 3" <> '') AND ("Group Level 3" <> GroupLevel.Code) THEN
                                    IF GroupLevel.GET("Group Level 3") THEN
                                      IF (GroupLevel.Description <> '') THEN
                                        GroupLevelTxt[3] := GroupLevel.Description;

                                  CLEAR(Amount);
                                  CLEAR(AmountBudget);
                                  CLEAR(AmountBudgetLevel1);
                                  CLEAR(AmountBudgetLevel2);
                                  CLEAR(AmountBudgetLevel3);
                                  CLEAR(AmountBudgetResult);
                                  CLEAR(AmountRev);

                                  Counter := 0;
                                  IF CostComponent.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                                    REPEAT
                                      Counter := Counter + 1;
                                      PlantType2.COPY(PlantType);
                                      PlantType2.SETFILTER("Cost Component Filter", CostComponent.Code);
                                      PlantType2.CALCFIELDS(Costs);
                                      Amount[Counter] := PlantType2.Costs;

                                      AmountBudget[Counter] := 0;
                                      AmountBudgetResult[Counter] := 0;
                                      IF PrintColBudgetPerCostComp THEN BEGIN
                                        CLEAR(PlantBudgetRubric);
                                        PlantBudgetRubric."Plant Budget" := PlantBudget.Code;
                                        PlantBudgetRubric."Plant Type" := Code;
                                        PlantBudgetRubric.Level := 4;
                                        AmountBudget[Counter] := PlantBudgetRubric.GetBudget(CostComponent.Code, PlantType.GETFILTER("Date Filter"));
                                        AmountBudgetResult[Counter] := AmountBudget[Counter] - Amount[Counter];

                                        PlantBudgetRubric."Plant Type" := PlantType."Group Level 1";
                                        PlantBudgetRubric.Level := 1;
                                        AmountBudgetLevel1[Counter] := PlantBudgetRubric.GetBudget(CostComponent.Code, PlantType.GETFILTER("Date Filter"));

                                        PlantBudgetRubric."Plant Type" := PlantType."Group Level 2";
                                        PlantBudgetRubric.Level := 2;
                                        AmountBudgetLevel2[Counter] := PlantBudgetRubric.GetBudget(CostComponent.Code, PlantType.GETFILTER("Date Filter"));

                                        PlantBudgetRubric."Plant Type" := PlantType."Group Level 3";
                                        PlantBudgetRubric.Level := 3;
                                        AmountBudgetLevel3[Counter] := PlantBudgetRubric.GetBudget(CostComponent.Code, PlantType.GETFILTER("Date Filter"));

                                        IF PrevGroupLevel1 <> "Group Level 1" THEN
                                          AmountBudgetResultLevel1[Counter] := AmountBudgetLevel1[Counter];
                                        IF PrevGroupLevel2 <> "Group Level 2" THEN
                                          AmountBudgetResultLevel2[Counter] := AmountBudgetLevel2[Counter];
                                        IF PrevGroupLevel3 <> "Group Level 3" THEN
                                          AmountBudgetResultLevel3[Counter] := AmountBudgetLevel3[Counter];

                                        AmountBudgetResultLevel1[Counter] -= Amount[Counter];
                                        AmountBudgetResultLevel2[Counter] -= Amount[Counter];
                                        AmountBudgetResultLevel3[Counter] -= Amount[Counter];
                                        AmountBudgetResultTotal[Counter] -= Amount[Counter];

                                        PrevGroupLevel1 := "Group Level 1";
                                        PrevGroupLevel2 := "Group Level 2";
                                        PrevGroupLevel3 := "Group Level 3";
                                      END;

                                      AmountRev[Counter] := 0;
                                      IF PrintColRevenues THEN BEGIN
                                        StandardRateComponent.SETRANGE("Cost Component", CostComponent.Code);
                                        IF StandardRateComponent.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                                          REPEAT
                                            PlantRateComponentEntry1.SETRANGE("Plant Type", Code);
                                            PlantRateComponentEntry1.SETRANGE("Rate Component", StandardRateComponent.Code);
                                            COPYFILTER("Gen. Bus. Posting Group Filter", PlantRateComponentEntry1."Gen. Bus. Posting Group");
                                            COPYFILTER("Posting Group Filter", PlantRateComponentEntry1."Plant Posting Group");
                                            COPYFILTER("Date Filter", PlantRateComponentEntry1."Posting Date");
                                            COPYFILTER("Revenue Filter", PlantRateComponentEntry1."Relate to");
                                            PlantRateComponentEntry1.CALCSUMS(Amount);
                                            AmountRev[Counter] := AmountRev[Counter] + PlantRateComponentEntry1.Amount;
                                          UNTIL StandardRateComponent.NEXT = 0;
                                        END;
                                      END;

                                      IF PrintCostAndRevOnSameLine THEN BEGIN
                                        Counter := Counter + 1;
                                        Amount[Counter] := AmountRev[Counter-1];
                                        AmountRev[Counter-1] := 0;
                                      END;
                                    UNTIL CostComponent.NEXT = 0;
                                  END;

                                  IF PrintColTotalCosts OR PrintColTotalBudget OR PrintColTotalRevenues OR PrintColResult THEN BEGIN
                                    PlantType2.COPY(PlantType);
                                    IF NOT OnlyTotalsOfSelectedCostComp THEN
                                      PlantType2.SETFILTER("Cost Component Filter", '');
                                    PlantType2.CALCFIELDS(Costs, Revenues);
                                  END;

                                  IF PrintColTotalCosts THEN
                                    Amount[ColNoTotalCosts] := PlantType2.Costs;

                                  IF PrintColTotalBudget THEN BEGIN
                                    CLEAR(PlantBudgetRubric);
                                    PlantBudgetRubric."Plant Budget" := PlantBudget.Code;
                                    PlantBudgetRubric."Plant Type" := Code;
                                    PlantBudgetRubric.Level := 4;
                                    IF NOT OnlyTotalsOfSelectedCostComp THEN
                                      Amount[ColNoTotalBudget] := PlantBudgetRubric.GetBudget('', PlantType.GETFILTER("Date Filter"))
                                    ELSE
                                      Amount[ColNoTotalBudget] := PlantBudgetRubric.GetBudget(PlantType.GETFILTER("Cost Component Filter"), PlantType.GETFILTER("Date Filter"));
                                    Amount[ColNoTotalBudgetResult] := Amount[ColNoTotalBudget] - PlantType2.Costs;
                                  END;

                                  IF PrintColTotalRevenues THEN
                                    Amount[ColNoTotalRevenues] := PlantType2.Revenues;

                                  IF PrintColResult THEN
                                    Amount[ColNoResult] := PlantType2.Revenues - PlantType2.Costs;

                                  IF PrintColOccupation THEN
                                    Amount[ColNoOccupation] := CalcOccupation.OccupationPercentage(PlantType, '', TotalNoOfDays, TotalNoOfRentalDays);

                                  AllZeroAmounts := TRUE;
                                  FOR Counter := 1 TO MaxNoColumns DO BEGIN
                                    IF Amount[Counter] <> 0 THEN
                                      AllZeroAmounts := FALSE;
                                    IF AmountBudget[Counter] <> 0 THEN
                                      AllZeroAmounts := FALSE;
                                    IF AmountRev[Counter] <> 0 THEN
                                      AllZeroAmounts := FALSE;
                                    AmountNotSpecified[Counter] := Amount[Counter];
                                    AmountRevNoNotSpecified[Counter] := AmountRev[Counter];
                                  END;

                                  IF (NOT PrintZeroLines) AND (AllZeroAmounts) THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=Code,Cost Component Filter,Revenue Filter,Date Filter,Gen. Bus. Posting Group Filter,Posting Group Filter }

    { 1100525065;1;Column;Code_PlantType     ;
               IncludeCaption=Yes;
               SourceExpr=PlantType.Code }

    { 1100525006;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012552;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Plant Type,No.);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF NOT PrintPerNo THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               PlantType.COPYFILTER("Date Filter", "Date Filter");
                               PlantType.COPYFILTER("Cost Component Filter", "Cost Component Filter");
                               PlantType.COPYFILTER("Revenue Filter", "Revenue Filter");
                               PlantType.COPYFILTER("Gen. Bus. Posting Group Filter", "Gen. Bus. Posting Group Filter");
                               PlantType.COPYFILTER("Posting Group Filter", "Posting Group Filter");
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  CLEAR(AmountPerNo);
                                  CLEAR(AmountBudgetPerNo);
                                  CLEAR(AmountBudgetResultPerNo);
                                  CLEAR(AmountRevPerNo);

                                  Counter := 0;
                                  IF CostComponent.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                                    REPEAT
                                      Counter := Counter + 1;
                                      PlantNo.COPY("Plant Number");
                                      PlantNo.SETFILTER("Cost Component Filter", CostComponent.Code);
                                      PlantNo.CALCFIELDS(Costs);
                                      AmountPerNo[Counter] := PlantNo.Costs;

                                      IF PrintColBudgetPerCostComp THEN BEGIN
                                        CLEAR(PlantBudgetRubric);
                                        PlantBudgetRubric.SETRANGE("Plant Budget", PlantBudget.Code);
                                        PlantBudgetRubric.SETRANGE("Plant Type", "Plant Type");
                                        PlantBudgetRubric.SETRANGE("Plant No.", "No.");
                                        IF PlantBudgetRubric.FINDFIRST THEN
                                          AmountBudgetPerNo[Counter] := PlantBudgetRubric.GetBudget(CostComponent.Code, PlantType.GETFILTER("Date Filter"));
                                        AmountBudgetResultPerNo[Counter] := AmountBudgetPerNo[Counter] - AmountPerNo[Counter];
                                      END;

                                      AmountRevPerNo[Counter] := 0;
                                      IF PrintColRevenues THEN BEGIN
                                        StandardRateComponent.SETRANGE("Cost Component", CostComponent.Code);
                                        IF StandardRateComponent.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                                          REPEAT
                                            PlantRateComponentEntry2.SETRANGE("Plant Type", "Plant Type" );
                                            PlantRateComponentEntry2.SETRANGE("Plant No.", "No.");
                                            PlantRateComponentEntry2.SETRANGE("Rate Component", StandardRateComponent.Code);
                                            COPYFILTER("Gen. Bus. Posting Group Filter", PlantRateComponentEntry2."Gen. Bus. Posting Group");
                                            COPYFILTER("Posting Group Filter", PlantRateComponentEntry2."Plant Posting Group");
                                            COPYFILTER("Date Filter", PlantRateComponentEntry2."Posting Date");
                                            COPYFILTER("Revenue Filter", PlantRateComponentEntry2."Relate to");
                                            PlantRateComponentEntry2.CALCSUMS(Amount);
                                            AmountRevPerNo[Counter] := AmountRevPerNo[Counter] + PlantRateComponentEntry2.Amount;
                                          UNTIL StandardRateComponent.NEXT = 0;
                                        END;
                                      END;

                                      IF PrintCostAndRevOnSameLine THEN BEGIN
                                        Counter := Counter + 1;
                                        AmountPerNo[Counter] := AmountRevPerNo[Counter-1];
                                        AmountRevPerNo[Counter-1] := 0;
                                      END;
                                    UNTIL CostComponent.NEXT = 0;
                                  END;

                                  IF PrintColTotalCosts OR PrintColTotalBudget OR PrintColTotalRevenues OR PrintColResult THEN BEGIN
                                    PlantNo.COPY("Plant Number");
                                    IF NOT OnlyTotalsOfSelectedCostComp THEN
                                      PlantNo.SETFILTER("Cost Component Filter", '');
                                    PlantNo.CALCFIELDS(Costs, Revenues);
                                  END;

                                  IF PrintColTotalCosts THEN
                                    AmountPerNo[ColNoTotalCosts] := PlantNo.Costs;

                                  IF PrintColTotalBudget THEN BEGIN
                                    CLEAR(PlantBudgetRubric);
                                    PlantBudgetRubric.SETRANGE("Plant Budget", PlantBudget.Code);
                                    PlantBudgetRubric.SETRANGE("Plant Type", "Plant Type");
                                    PlantBudgetRubric.SETRANGE("Plant No.", "No.");
                                    IF PlantBudgetRubric.FINDFIRST THEN
                                      IF NOT OnlyTotalsOfSelectedCostComp THEN
                                        AmountPerNo[ColNoTotalBudget] := PlantBudgetRubric.GetBudget('', PlantType.GETFILTER("Date Filter"))
                                      ELSE
                                        AmountPerNo[ColNoTotalBudget] := PlantBudgetRubric.GetBudget(PlantType.GETFILTER("Cost Component Filter"), PlantType.GETFILTER("Date Filter"));
                                    AmountPerNo[ColNoTotalBudgetResult] := AmountPerNo[ColNoTotalBudget] - PlantNo.Costs;
                                  END;

                                  IF PrintColTotalRevenues THEN
                                    AmountPerNo[ColNoTotalRevenues] := PlantNo.Revenues;

                                  IF PrintColResult THEN
                                    AmountPerNo[ColNoResult] := PlantNo.Revenues - PlantNo.Costs;

                                  IF PrintColOccupation THEN
                                    AmountPerNo[ColNoOccupation] := 0; //* Occupation is not calculated on Plant No. level!

                                  AllZeroAmounts := TRUE;
                                  FOR Counter := 1 TO MaxNoColumns DO BEGIN
                                    IF AmountPerNo[Counter] <> 0 THEN
                                      AllZeroAmounts := FALSE;
                                    IF AmountBudgetPerNo[Counter] <> 0 THEN
                                      AllZeroAmounts := FALSE;
                                    IF AmountRevPerNo[Counter] <> 0 THEN
                                      AllZeroAmounts := FALSE;
                                    AmountNotSpecified[Counter] := AmountNotSpecified[Counter] - AmountPerNo[Counter];
                                    AmountRevNoNotSpecified[Counter] := AmountRevNoNotSpecified[Counter] - AmountRevPerNo[Counter];
                                  END;

                                  IF (NOT PrintZeroLines) AND (AllZeroAmounts) THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Plant Type=FIELD(Code) }

    { 1100525073;2;Column;PlantType_PlantNumber;
               SourceExpr="Plant Number"."Plant Type" }

               SourceExpr="Plant Number"."No." }

                   ELSE

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetReportFilter@1100525000() : Text;
    BEGIN
      IF PlantType.GETFILTERS <> '' THEN
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2', PlantType.TABLECAPTION, PlantType.GETFILTERS));
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckDiffBetweenNosAndType@1210190002() : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      FOR Counter := 1 TO MaxNoColumns DO BEGIN
        IF (Counter <> ColNoOccupation) AND
           ((AmountNotSpecified[Counter] <> 0) OR (AmountRevNoNotSpecified[Counter] <> 0)) THEN
          EXIT(TRUE);
      END;

      EXIT(FALSE);
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      Attention: On groupinglevel, you can also enter/create a budget.

      AmountBudgetLevel will be passed for each planttype record in dataset, because there is no dataitem for groupinglevel.
      You can't totalize this in the report, because this total amount will become to high.
      There is a seperate dataitem for the total of all levels.

      AmountBudgetResultLevel can't be calculated in the report (by AmountBudgetLevel - Sum(AmountBudget)) because you don't know
      if it concerns a column of one of the cost components. So also for this there are seperate fields in dataset.
    }
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function CalcGroupTotal(ColNo As Integer, ColNoOccupation As Integer, SumValue As Double, NoOfDays As Integer, NoOfRentalDays As Integer) As Double
    If ColNo &lt;&gt; ColNoOccupation Then
        Return SumValue
    Else
        If NoOfDays = 0 Then
            Return 0
        Else
            Return (NoOfRentalDays / NoOfDays) * 100
        End If
    End If
End Function

Public Function CalcBudgetResult(ColNo As Integer, CostComponentColCount As Integer, ResultValue As Double) As Double
    If ColNo &lt;= CostComponentColCount Then
        Return ResultValue
    Else
        Return 0      
    End If
End Function

Shared TotalPrinted As Boolean

Public Function LastRowIsTotal(ByVal Value As Boolean) As Boolean
    If TotalPrinted = False Then
        TotalPrinted = Value
        Return False
    End If
    If TotalPrinted = True Then
        TotalPrinted = Value
        Return True
    End If
End Function
